Approximately 75kms, the yatra begins at the Manikarnika Ghat, then Shri Kardameshwar Mahadev, Devi Bheem Chandi, Rameshwar Mahadev, Pancha Pandava, and Kapil Dhara. \r\nThen the yatris go to Jau Vinayak and a steamer takes them back to Manikarnika.\r\nWomen undertake a 5 days Parikrama in the month of Malmas.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nHome\n\nKashi Panchkoshi Parikrama \n\nKashi Panchkoshi Parikrama\nKardameshwar Mahadev\nBheem Chandi\nRameshwar Mahadev\nPanch Pandava\nKapil Dhara\n\n\n\nGalleries \n\nKardameshwar Mahadev\nBheem Chandi Gallery\nRameshwar Gallery\nKapil Dhara\n\n\n\nMandirs \n\nShri Adi Keshava Mandir\nMarkandeya Mahadev,Kaithi\nBhairav Nath Mandir\nDindaspur, Harsos, Jansa\nPahadia Mandir, Akhara and Sarovar\n\n\n\nGhats\nFestivals\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nDevi Bhim Chandi Mandir\nSecond stop on the Panch Koshi parikrama.\n\n\n\n\n\nView of the Ganga from Lalita Ghat\nBoats in the Ganga in Varanasi.\n\n\n\n\n\nApproach to Devi Bhim Chandi Mandir\nSecond stop on the Panch Koshi parikrama.\n\n\n\n\n\nRameshwar Mahadev Mandir\nRameshwar Mahadev Mandir, Ganga-Varuna Sangam Varanasi.\n\n\n\n\n\nKapil Dhara Mandir\nKapil Dhara Mandir, last stop on the Kashi Panchkoshi Parikrama\n\n\n\n\n\nPancha Pandava Mandir\nPancha Pandava Mandir, fourth stop on the Kashi Panchkoshi Parikrama\n\n\n\n\n\nBoats on the Ganga\nBoats near the Ganga Ghats\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrevious\n\n\n\nNext\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAbout the Panchkoshi Parikrama \n\r\n The Panchkoshi Kshetra in Varanasi is described in the Skanda Purana in these words:\r\n "Though it is on the earth, it has no contact with it.\r\n Being higher than the heavens, yet it is established on the earth.\r\n Even though it is made of the five elements it gives Moksha to everyone.\r\n Everyone who dies here becomes immortal Brahmas.\r\n That which is renowned in the 3 Lokas as the city on the bank of the Ganga. It is the holiest city for Hindus. It is the Avimukta Kshetra where Purusha and Prakriti dwelt first. Varanasi is Shiva KShetra. It was a Vishnu KShetra before. \r\n Varanasi is settle next to the left banks of the Ganga and numerous Ghats line up their. Varanasi is also the dwelling place of Shiva where he lives as the Vishweshwar Linga in the Kashi Viswanath Mandir at Gyanvapi.\r\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe Assi River\nThe Assi River flows into the Ganga at the famous Assi Ghat. The Assi Ghat is famous as the dwelling place of Goswami Tulsidas ji.\r\n The Ramacharita Manas was composed here. The Assi Ghat is famous for the early morning Kirtans and cultural activities. The Ganga Aarti takes place here.\r\n The Assi River flows next to the Baba Kinarama Asthal. The river has unfortunately been polluted beyond recognition by sewers emptying into it.\r\n Efforts are being made to revive it.\r\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\nPlaces in Varanasi\n\n\n\n\nBheem Chandi\nBheem Chandi,Rameshwar\n\n\n\n\n\nRameshwar Mahadev Mandir on the Varuna\nThird stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama\n\n\n\n\n\nKapil Dhara, Varanasi\nLast stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama Yatra\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nBhairav Nath Mandir.\nOn the Rajatalab to Jansa Road\n\n\n\n\n\nPancha Pandava Mandir, Varanasi\n fourth stop on the Kashi Panchkoshi parikrama.\n\n\n\n\n\nKapil Dhara, Varanasi\nFifth and last stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nMap of Varanasi\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCONTACT\n\n\nContact us for any query about Varanasi and we'll get back to you within 24 hours.\n Varanasi, India\n +91 9335874326\n varanasikshetra@gmail.com\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSend\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nÂ©Champak's World\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n NaN NaN NaN

The Ganga Aarti takes place here.\r\n The Assi River flows next to the Baba Kinarama Asthal. The river has unfortunately been polluted beyond recognition by sewers emptying into it.\r\n Efforts are being made to revive it.\r\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\nPlaces in Varanasi\n\n\n\n\nBheem Chandi\nBheem Chandi,Rameshwar\n\n\n\n\n\nRameshwar Mahadev Mandir on the Varuna\nThird stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama\n\n\n\n\n\nKapil Dhara, Varanasi\nLast stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama Yatra\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nBhairav Nath Mandir.\nOn the Rajatalab to Jansa Road\n\n\n\n\n\nPancha Pandava Mandir, Varanasi\n fourth stop on the Kashi Panchkoshi parikrama.\n\n\n\n\n\nKapil Dhara, Varanasi\nFifth and last stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama\n\n\n\n\n NaN NaN
